## Domain Knowledge
**Domain**: population ecology / population dynamics
**Analysis**: This task involves modeling population growth rate (dP/dt) as a function of time (t) and current population (P). This is a classic population dynamics problem where growth rate depends on population size through various density-dependent and density-independent mechanisms.

**Common formula structures** (built-in generic + LLM domain-specific):
- Arrhenius equation: k = c0 * exp(c1 / T) (chemical reaction rate dependence on temperature)
- Coulomb's / Newton's inverse-square law: F = c0 / r**2 (gravitational or electrostatic force)
- Stefan-Boltzmann law: P = c0 * T**4 (blackbody radiation power vs temperature)
- Beer-Lambert law: I = c0 * exp(c1 * x) (light intensity attenuation through a medium)
- Michaelis-Menten kinetics: v = c0 * S / (S + c1) (enzyme-catalyzed reaction saturation)
- Hill equation: y = c0 * x**c1 / (x**c1 + c2) (cooperative binding, sigmoidal dose-response)
- Kepler's third law: T**2 = c0 * a**3 (orbital period vs semi-major axis)
- Newton's law of cooling: T = c0 + c1 * exp(c2 * t) (exponential thermal relaxation)
- Clausius-Clapeyron relation: log(P) = c0 + c1 / T (vapor pressure vs temperature)
- Langmuir adsorption isotherm: theta = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P) (surface adsorption equilibrium)
- Freundlich isotherm: q = c0 * C**c1 (empirical adsorption on heterogeneous surface)
- Stokes' drag: F = c0 * r * v (viscous drag force on a sphere in fluid)
- Logistic growth: N = c0 / (1 + c1 * exp(c2 * t)) (population dynamics with carrying capacity)
- Planck-Wien approximation: I = c0 * f**3 * exp(c1 * f / T) (thermal radiation spectrum)
- {'name': 'Exponential (Malthusian) growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P', 'scenario': 'Density-independent growth where rate is proportional to population size'}
- {'name': 'Logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Density-dependent growth with carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Gompertz growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * log(c1 / P)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate decreasing logarithmically as population approaches carrying capacity'}
- {'name': 'Theta-logistic growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2)', 'scenario': 'Generalized logistic with nonlinear density dependence'}
- {'name': 'Allee effect growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (P - c1) * (1 - c2 * P)', 'scenario': 'Growth with minimum viable population threshold (strong Allee effect)'}
- {'name': 'Richards growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - (c1 * P)**c2) / c2', 'scenario': 'Flexible asymmetric sigmoidal growth model'}
- {'name': 'Power-law density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1', 'scenario': 'Growth rate as a power function of population'}
- {'name': 'Beverton-Holt continuous form', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P / (1 + c1 * P)', 'scenario': 'Saturating growth rate with contest competition'}
- {'name': 'Time-dependent exponential growth', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * exp(c1 * t)', 'scenario': 'Growth rate with time-varying intrinsic rate'}
- {'name': 'Logistic with time-varying capacity', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P * (1 - c1 * P * exp(c2 * t))', 'scenario': 'Logistic growth where carrying capacity changes over time'}
- {'name': 'Quadratic density dependence', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P + c1 * P**2 + c2 * P**3', 'scenario': 'Polynomial expansion of density-dependent effects'}
- {'name': 'Von Bertalanffy-type growth rate', 'formula': 'dP_dt = c0 * P**c1 - c2 * P', 'scenario': 'Balance between anabolic (power-law) and catabolic (linear) processes'}

**Formula structure heuristic features**:
- Oscillation damping envelope â†’ Exponential decay envelope f(x)*exp(-c*Abs(x)) for symmetric damped oscillation, Gaussian envelope f(x)*exp(-c*x**2) for localized wave packets
- Saturation/clipping effects â†’ Rational fraction x/(1+x), tanh; for variables with alternating positive/negative in oscillatory systems, selectively apply Abs
- Growth/decay â†’ Exponential growth exp(c*t), Logistic 1/(1+exp(-c*x)), power law x**c
- Threshold/activation behavior â†’ Max(x-c, 0), piecewise functions
- Coupling/cross effects â†’ Product terms between variables x*y, power-law coupling x**c1 * y**c2
- Density-dependent negative feedback â†’ quadratic term -c*P^2 in growth rate (logistic-type self-limitation)
- Allee effect / positive density dependence at low P â†’ cubic polynomial in P with sign changes creating multiple equilibria
- Carrying capacity behavior â†’ growth rate crosses zero at finite P, implying factored form P*(K-P)
- Gompertz-type asymmetry â†’ logarithmic dependence log(K/P) giving slower approach to carrying capacity from above vs below
- Time-explicit dependence in autonomous ODE â†’ suggests environmental forcing or non-stationary conditions, often multiplicative with P-dependent terms
- Fractional power of P â†’ indicates allometric scaling of metabolic or reproductive rates with body/population size
- Ratio-dependent terms P/(P+c) â†’ interference or handling time effects in resource acquisition limiting per-capita growth
- Sign of dP_dt changing with P â†’ indicates equilibrium points; number of sign changes reveals number of stable/unstable equilibria
